1a1(mdo sde): rgyal pos bsgyur bar mdzad pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ba bsgrub pa'i don
1a2(mdo sde): mngon par thob pa'i rgyu/byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi spyod pa rgya mtsho ston pa/sangs
1a3(mdo sde): rgyas kyi gtsug tor dpa' bar 'gro ba zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo//bam po bcu pa//
1b1(mdo sde): rgya gar skad du/sarba ta thA ga ta s+ya guh+ya sid+d+hen+da A b+hi sa ma ya he tu sarba bo d+ha/
1b2(mdo sde): satwA s+ya tsar+ya sa mu tA daM sha bud+d+hoSh+TaM She shA rang+ga nA me ma hA yA no sU tA/bod skad du/de bzhin
1b3(mdo sde): gshegs pa'i gsang ba bsgrub pa'i don mngon par thob pa'i rgyu/byang chub sems dpa'
1b4(mdo sde): thams cad kyi spyod pa rgya mtsho ston pa/sangs rgyas kyi gtsug tor dpa' bar 'gro ba zhes bya ba theg
2a1(mdo sde): pa chen po'i mdo//bam po dang po//'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na
2a2(mdo sde): rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na/stong nyis brgya lnga bcu'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang
2a3(mdo sde): thabs gcig tu bzhugs so//thams cad kyang dgra bcom pa/zag pa zad pa/shAkya'i sras po ches la dbang thob pa/srid pa thams
2a4(mdo sde): cad las rnam par grol ba/grong khyer gyi skye bo la sman par mdzad pa/sangs rgyas dang lhan cig chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba/chos kyi tshul
2a5(mdo sde): ston par nus pa/'dul ba'i tshul gtsang po/khams gsum las 'phags pa'i spobs pa can/rdzu 'phrul dpag tu med pa/gdul bya
2b1(mdo sde): sgrol bar byed pa/ma 'ongs pa'i 'gro ba 'dren pa/sdug bsngal gyi 'obs las brgal ba sha stag la 'di lta ste/gtso bor gyur pa ni/nyan thos chen po shA ri'i bu
2b2(mdo sde): dang mau t+pal gyi bu chen po dang /gsus po che dang /gang po byams ma'i bu dang /rab 'byor dang nye rgyal sogs nyan thos chen po rnams dang /gzhan yang rang rgyal
2b3(mdo sde): slob pa dang mi slob pa'i dge 'dun dang /gsar du zhugs pa'i nyan thos grangs med pa rnams dang lhan cig tu/dbyar gnas pa las dgag dbye'i dus su phyogs
2b4(mdo sde): bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyang the tshom gcod pa'i slad du/bcom ldan 'das la chos ston par gsol bar lhags nas/bcom ldan 'das la
2b5(mdo sde): thugs brtse bas rjes su gdams pa dang /gsang ba'i gnas yongs su zhu bar 'khod pa na bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi gsang ba 'di 'chad par mdzad pa'i phyir
2b6(mdo sde): gdan bshams pa la sku drang por bsrang nas bzhugs te/'khor 'dus pa rnams kyis thos par dka' ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba 'di/
3a1(mdo sde): gsung ka la ping+ga'i dbyangs kyis phyogs bcur khyab par mdzad de ston par mdzad do//de'i tshe gang+ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
3a2(mdo sde): kyang 'dus par gyur te/byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal dbyangs gtso bor gyur pa'o//dus de'i tshe rgyal po gsal rgyal gyis rang gi yab kyi dus mchod bya ba'i phyir
3a3(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das la gdugs tshad gsol bar pho brang du gdan drangs so//rang nyid kyis bsus te/zhal zas bla na med pa'i ro mchog dang ldan pa rgya chen po bshams/byang
3a4(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' rnams kyang thabs gcig tu gdan drangs shing pho brang gi bram ze dang rig byed mkhas pa rnams kyang dus ston la mgron du gnyer ro//de dag thams cad kyis
3a5(mdo sde): kyang bcom ldan 'das rang rang gi gnas su dus ston gsol bar 'dod pa na/bcom ldan 'das kyis 'jam dpal dbyangs la bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis byang chub sems
3a6(mdo sde): dpa' rnams dang dgra bcom pa rnams la sbyin bdag gi khyim so sor dus ston spyod par byed du chug shig gsung ngo //kun dga' bo ni snga logs shig nas gzhan zhig tu phyin
3b1(mdo sde): nas dus ston der ma 'dus pa las re shig na gnas brtan dang slob dpon gzhan med par/rang nyid gcig pur 'ongs pa na/gdugs tshod yol bas lhung bzed thogs te/bsod snyoms
3b2(mdo sde): la khyim nas khyim du rgyu ba na/'di snyam du sems te/bdag gis ci nas kyang sbyin bdag mchog gam dman pa yang rung ste/rgyal rigs dang /gdol pa'i rigs sogs gtsang ba dang /smad
3b3(mdo sde): pa mtha' dag snyoms par sems pas/sbyin pa po mtha' dag gi dge ba dpag tu med pa rdzogs par bya'o//ci'i phyir na/bcom ldan 'das kyis 'od srung chen po dang /rab 'byor la 'di
3b4(mdo sde): skad ces nyan thos chen po khyed cag gis sems mi snyoms pa ma byed cig ces nan tar bzlog par mdzad pas so//zhes sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa la brten te sems kyi sgrib pa bsal te the
3b5(mdo sde): tshom dang smad par 'gyur ba'i gnas spangs te/lam srang mthar gyis bgrod nas pho brang gi sgor sleb pa na gzugs drang por bsrang ste/dran pa mngon du byas nas/slong ba'i spyod lam zhi bas rgyu
3b6(mdo sde): ba'i tshe/smad 'tshong ma'i sgo khang du sleb pa na/sgyu ma'i g.yo thabs kyi 'phrul can/ma taM gi dang phrad pa na des ka pi la zhes bya ba'i tshangs pa'i rig sngags btab pas kun dga' bo rang dbang med
3b7(mdo sde): par rig sngags kyis gzir te rjes su 'brang nas/khang par sleb pa na nom nyug byed par brtsams shing /mi tshangs par spyod par byed pa na/bcom ldan 'das kyis kun dga' bo sgyu ma'i sngags rdzas
4a1(mdo sde): kyis gzir ba mngon par mkhyen nas/bla'u zhal zas gsol te/phyir gshegs so//de'i tshe rgyal po dang blon po dang khyim bdag dang rje rigs rnams 'dus te/bcom
4a2(mdo sde): ldan 'das las chos nyan pa'i phyir slad kyis 'brangs pa na/bcom ldan 'das kyi spyi bo'i gtsug nas 'jigs pa med pa'i nor bu brgyang zhes bya ba'i 'od zer spros pa'i rtse mor pad+ma 'dab ma stong
4a3(mdo sde): dang ldan pa zhig byung ba la sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa'i gzugs dkyil krung gis bzhugaso pas gsang sngags kyi tshig bka' stsal to//de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/'jam dpal
4a4(mdo sde): khyod kyis rig sngags 'dis kun dga' bo bskyab par gyis la sgyu ma'i sngags rdzas 'jig par gyis shig gsungs pa dang /'jam dpal gyis bka' ji lta ba bzhin bgyis pas/ma ti gi dang
4a5(mdo sde): kun dga' bo yang 'jam dpal gyi slad bzhin bcom ldan 'das ga la bar 'ongs pa dang /kun dga' bos bcom ldan 'das mthong ba dang phyag 'tshal te mchi ma blags nas/ji ltar na bdag sngon
4a6(mdo sde): nas mang du thos pa lags na'ang rtogs pa'i chos kyi ro ma myong snyam du 'gyod pas gdungs bzhin du gus pa chen pos nan tar gsol ba/phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi byang chub
4a7(mdo sde): mngon du mdzad pa'i ni lhag gi ting nge 'dzin phul du byung ba bde blag tu 'thob pa'i thabs bshad du gsol/zhes nus pa dang /de'i tshe gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' dang /gzhan
4b1(mdo sde): yang phyogs bcu'i nyan thos chen po dang rang sangs rgyas kyi rigs la zhugs pa mang po dag kyang chos ston pa nyan par 'dod pas mchis shing /rna ba blags te cang mi smra bar 'khod do//bcom ldan 'das kyis
4b2(mdo sde): kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/khyod bdag dang rigs gcig pa lags te/sngon chad khyod kyis kho bos bstan pa'i tshul la legs pa ci zhig mthong nas drin dang ldan zhing snying du sdug pa dang phangs
4b3(mdo sde): pa dag bor nas rab tu byung bar gyur/kun dga' bos gsol ba/kho bos bcom ldan 'das kyi mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis kyis spras pa/ngo mtshar zhing dag cing gsal ba gzhan las khyad par du 'phags/
4b4(mdo sde): pa mthong nas rtag tu 'di ltar sems lags te/bai DUr+ya ltar rnam par dag pa'i sku'i bkod pa 'di ni 'dod pa dang sred pa'i zag pa dang 'dres pa ma yin te/ci'i phyir zhe na/'dod pa dang sred pa ni dri ma
4b5(mdo sde): dang snyigs ma mi gtsang bas sbrel ba/khru khrag 'dres pa las ni ngo mtshar zhing khyad par du 'phags pa gser bcom lta bu'i dag cing gsal ba'i sku'i bkod pa de lta bu 'khrungs par mi rigs so//de
4b6(mdo sde): bas na rgyu 'dis sems gus pas dad cing skra bregs te khyod kyi rjes su rab tu byung ba lags/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/legs so//kun dga' bo/khyed cag gis 'di ltar blta
4b7(mdo sde): ste/thog ma med pa nas skye 'chi gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas 'khor ba na rang gi de kho na nyid dag cing 'od gsal ba rtag tu gnas pa ma rtogs pas mngon zhe na nye bar blangs te/'dod pa 'di
5a1(mdo sde): ni gsog 'ba' zhig pas na kun tu rgyud mar 'khor zhing 'phyan to//khyod da ste bla na med pa'i byang chub don dam pa'i de kho na nyid nan tan du 'tshol bar sems na rnam par dag
5a2(mdo sde): pa'i yid kyis lan smos shig/phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyang bgrod pa gcig pa'i dbu ma'i lam 'dis skye 'chi brgal ba ste/sems dang ngag dbu ma'i lam du gnas pa'i
5a3(mdo sde): phyir ro//mthar thug pa'i bar gyi sa dang lam la gnas pa thams cad kyang dbu ma'i lam 'di las rnam pa gzhan du 'dren pa ma mchis so//kun dga' bo/kho bos khyod la dri bar bya ste/khyod kyis
5a4(mdo sde): dang por de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis la sems na ji ltar na mtshan bzang por blta bar bya/gang gis na blta bar bya/kun dga' bos gsol pa/ston pa/kho bos mig
5a5(mdo sde): dang yid kyis mthong zhing 'dod pa ste/mig gis gsal bar bcom ldan 'das kyi sku khyad par du 'phags pa mthong ba las yid kyis mngon par 'dod pa lags so//de ltar na bdag gis skye 'chi/
5a6(mdo sde): spangs par 'khums lags so//bcom ldan 'das kyis kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis mig gis mthong zhing yid kyis 'dod na/mig dang yid gang la gnas pa ma shes na nyon mong/
5a7(mdo sde): dang sdug bsngal spangs par mi nus te/dper na rgyal po 'ga' zhig chom po pa 'ongs pa dmag gis bzlog par 'dod pa na dmag gi dpung des kyang chom po pa gang du gnas pa shes par bya dgos pa
5b1(mdo sde): bzhin no//mig dang yid dag nyid kyis 'khor bar bsdam pa ste/mig dang yid dag nyid gang du gnas pa khyod la dri bar bya'o//kun dga' bos gsol ba/ston pa 'khor ba'i sems can thams cad sems can
5b2(mdo sde): du gdags pa'i rnam grangs bcus bsdus pa so so ba nyid na'ang de dag thams cad kyis rnam par shes pa lus kyi nang du gnas par blta'o//bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan mthon mthing pad+ma lta bu yang zhal gyi dkyil
5b3(mdo sde): 'khor du mchis par blta'o//bdag gi yul bzhi 'dzin pa'i dbang po gzugs can dngas pa bzhi ni bdag gi gzugs nyid la gnas ste/bdag gi rnam par shes pa ni lus kyi nang du gnas par blta lags
5b4(mdo sde): so/bcom ldan 'das kyis kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/da lta khyod sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi 'dun sar gnas pa na rgyal byed kyi tshal gang du gnas par blta/kun dga' bos gsol pa/ston pa chos kyi
5b5(mdo sde): 'dun sa rnam par dag pa'i kun dga' ra ba 'di ni mgon med zas sbyin gyi gnas lags te/rgyal byed kyi tshal ni phyi logs su mchis so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/kun dga' bo/khyod kyis
5b6(mdo sde): chos kyi 'dun sa 'dir je ci zhig mthong /kun dga' bos gsol pa/ston pa bdag gi je bcom ldan 'das dang de nas dge 'dun dang phyi logs su kun dga' ra ba tshal dang bcas pa mthong ngo //bcom ldan
5b7(mdo sde): 'das kyis kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/kun dga' bo ji ltar na khyod kyis kun dga' ra ba tshal dang bcas pa mthong ba yin/kun dga' bos gsol ba/ston pa kun dga' ra ba gseng yab dang mthong rgya
6a1(mdo sde): //che ba 'di'i nang du bdag gnas bzhin du mthong ngo //de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis phyag gser gyi mdog can brkyang ste 'khor 'dus pa'i nang nas kun dga' bo'i spyi bor bzhag ste/'khor
6a2(mdo sde): 'dus pa rnams la bka' stsal pa/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gtsug tor dpa' bar 'gro ba'i rgyal po spyod pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin yod de/phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs
6a3(mdo sde): pa thams cad ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i lam 'di nyid dang sgo 'di nyid nas mngon par gshegs pa yin no//khyod kyis legs par nyon cig gsungs pas/kun dga' bos phyag 'tshal te gus pas 'dud cing 'dug
6a4(mdo sde): go bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis kun dga' ra ba gseng yab dang mthong rgya che ba 'di'i nang du gnas bzhin du phyi'i kun dga' ra ba nags tshal dang bcas pa mthong bar smran/ci sems can
6a5(mdo sde): 'ga' zhig 'dir gnas bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa ma mthong bar kun dga' ra ba'i phyi logs mthong ba lta mchis sam/kun dga' bos gsol ba/ston pa sems can 'ga' zhig 'drir gnas bzhin du//
6a6(mdo sde): debazhin gshegs pa ma mthong bar kun dga' ra ba'i phyi logs mthong ba 'ga' yang ma mchis so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/kun dga' bo khyod nyid de kho na yin te/khyod kyis rnam par shes
6a7(mdo sde): pagasal ba nyid na thams cad gsal bar rigs te/khyod kyi rnam par shes pa gsal ba lus kyi nang na lha mchis sam/de ltan lus kyi nang nyid gsal bar rigs na/sems can gyi nang na 'ga' zhig
6b1(mdo sde): thog mar shes pas lus kyi nang gsal bar byas nas gzod phyi'i yo byad gsal bar byed pa 'ga' mchis sam/ji ltar na snying mchin pa mcher ba pho ba lta zhog/sen mo dang skra'i khams dang chu rgyus dang /
6b2(mdo sde): rgyus g.yo ba yang mi gsal bar snang bzhin du shes pa nyid gsal bar 'gyur/ji ltar na de dag gsal bar mi 'gyur/des na nges par nang gsal ba nyid ma yin na/phyi gsal ba nyid du lta ga la 'gyur/des
6b3(mdo sde): na 'di ltar rtogs par bya ste/khyod kyis rnam par shes pa gsal zhing rig pa lus kyi nang du yod par smras pa ni gnas med pa'o//kun dga' bos phyag 'tshal te/bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba/bdag gis/
6b4(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das la chos kyi dbyangs 'di 'tshal ba lta na/gdon mi za bar rnam par shes pa ni lus kyi phyi na gnas par 'khums lags te/ci'i slad du na/dper na khang pa'i phugs su sbar ba'i sgron me nang
6b5(mdo sde): gsal ba nyid kyis sgo nas 'khyams tshar gsal bar byed do//sems can thams cad kyis nang gi bdag nyid mi gsal bar lus kyi phyi rol gsal ba ni yang mar me'i 'od kyis phyi'i dngos po gsal bar byed
6b6(mdo sde): kyi nang gi dngos po ma yin pa bzhin no//'di ni nges par/'di lta ste/gdon mi za bar ston pa'i dgongs pa la 'babs par 'gyur ba kho na lags sam/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis/
6b7(mdo sde): gang nga'i rjes su 'brang ste mnyan yod nas kham gyi zas bsod snyoms la rgyu bas rgyal byed kyi tshal du zas spangs pa'i dge slong la ltos shig/cig cig gis 'tshal ma 'tshal bas thams cad bgrangs
7a1(mdo sde): /par 'gyur logs sam/kun dga' bos gsol ba/ston pa de ltar ma lags so//ci'i slad du na/dge slong 'di dag dge slong nyid du mtshungs na'ang lus dang srog tha dad pa lags pas
7a2(mdo sde): ji ltar na gcig gis 'tshal ma 'tshal bas thams cad 'grangs par 'gyur/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/rnam par shes pa gsal zhing rig pa phyi rol du mchis ni lus dang sems tha dad
7a3(mdo sde): pas 'brel pa med par 'gyur la/sems nyid kyis mthong ba na lus kyis myong bar mi 'gyur la/lus nyid kyis myong ba na sems kyis rtogs par mi 'gyur ro//bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag shing bal ltar
7a4(mdo sde): 'jam pa 'di mthong na khyod kyi sems bye brag phyed par 'gyur ram/kun dga' bos gsol ba/ston pa de ltar lags so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/de ltar na rnam par shes pa ji ltar phyi/
7a5(mdo sde): rol du mchis zhes bya/des na 'di ltar rtogs par bya ste khyod kyis rnam par shes pa lus kyi phyi rol du gnas par smras pa 'di ni gnas med pa'o//kun dga' bos gsol pa/ston pa'i bka' stsal pa
7a6(mdo sde): ltar na/lus kyi nang nyid gsal ba ma yin pas na sems nang du mi gnas la/lus sems phan tshun du 'brel zhing /mi 'bral bas na sems lus kyi phyi rol du yang ma mchis te/bdag gis 'tshal ba
7a7(mdo sde): ltar na gnas pa'i gnas gcig mchis lags so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/gang du gnas par blta/kun dga' bos gsol pa/shes pa gsal zhing rig pa nang du yang ma yin
7b1(mdo sde): kyang phyi rol mthong nus pa las na/bdag gis 'tshal ba ltar na khams kyi nang du gab pa ste/dper na 'ga' zhig gis bai DUr+ya'i kong bu mig gnyis la bkab par gyur kyang snang yul la sgrib pa med pa bzhin du dbang
7b2(mdo sde): po des mthong bar gyur la bye brag phyed par 'gyur ro//rnam par shes pa gsal zhing rig pa lus kyi nang gsal ba ma yin pas na khams kyi nang du gnas shing /phyi rol rnam par gsal bar byed pa la mi sgrib pas na
7b3(mdo sde): dbang po'i sbubs na gab cing gnas so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyi smras pa ltar mig gi dbang po'i sbubs su bai DUr+ya'i kong bu mchis na/'on te mi 'ga' zhig bai DUr+ya'i kong bus mig 'gebs
7b4(mdo sde): bzhin blta ba na ri klung mtha' dag mthong bas tsi bai DUr+ya'i kong bu nyid mthong bar 'gyur ram mi 'gyur//kun dga' bos gsol ba/de lta lags te/bai DUr+ya nyid kyang mthong lags so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
7b5(mdo sde): stsal pa/sems bai DUr+ya'i kong bu dang mtshungs pa lta na ri klung mtha' dag mthong ba bzhin du mig nyid kyang ci'i phyir mi mthong /gal te mig nyid kyang mthong na ni mig nyid yul du 'gyur ste/'brel ba med par/
7b6(mdo sde): 'gyur ro//mig nyid mi mthong na ni ji ltar na dbang po'i sbubs su gnas shing bai DUr+ya'i kong bu dang mtshungs par 'gyur/des na 'di ltar rtogs par bya ste/khyod kyis rnam par shes pa gsal zhing rig pa khams
7b7(mdo sde): kyi nang du gnas shing bai DUr+ya'i kong bu dang mtshungs par smras pa 'di ni gnas med do//kun dga' bos gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das bdag gis yang 'di ltar sems te/sems can gyi lus don dang snod nang
8a1(mdo sde): na gnas shing sgo dang sbubs ni phyi rol du mchis la/nang na gnas pas mun par red la/phyin gnas pas gsal ba ste/bdag gis bcom ldan 'das kyi thad nas mig phye
8a2(mdo sde): ste bltas pa'i tshe gsal bar mthong ba nyid la phyi rol gsal bar bsnyad la/mig btsums pa na mun pa mthong ba nyid la nang gsal bar bsnyad pa ste/ci 'di lta bu yin lags sam/bcom
8a3(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/mig btsums pas mun pa mthong ba na mun pa'i khams dang mig 'phrad dam/ma 'phrad pa zhig yin grang 'on te 'phrad na ni mun pa nyid mig gi mdun rol du snang
8a4(mdo sde): bar 'gyur bas ji ltar na nang du gnas par 'gyur/ji ste nang du gnas na ni de'i tshe/mun pa 'thug po'i phug nyi ma dang zla ba dang mar me'i snang ba mi 'jug pa'i mun pa de nyid kyang khyod kyi nang rol dang
8a5(mdo sde): 'dra bar nyid du 'gyur/gal te ma 'phyang na ni ji ltar na mthong bar 'gyur/phyi rol mthong ba dang bral bas na nang gi bdag nyid 'phrad pas grub pa mig btsums pas mun pa mthong bas/lus kyi
8a6(mdo sde): nang mthong bar bsnyad la/mig phye ba'i tshe snang ba mthong na ci'i phyir byad bzhin mi mthong bar 'gyur/bzhin mi mthong ba zhig na nad bdag nyid dang 'phrad par 'gyur ba mi 'thad do//bzhin mthong
8a7(mdo sde): ba nyid na rnam shes gsal zhing rig pa mig gi khams dang bcas pa phyi rol gyi bar snang nyid du 'gyur gyi nang gi bdag nyid du mi 'brel bar 'gyur ro//'on te phyi rol gyi bar snang na yod pa zhig na//
8b1(mdo sde): rang gi lus dang mi 'brel par 'gyur la/bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang khyod kyi bzhin mthong bas ci khyod kyi lus dang 'brel bar 'gyur ba zhig gam/khyod kyis mig gis mthong ba tsam du 'gyur gyi khyod
8b2(mdo sde): nyid kyis ci yang mi shes par 'gyur ro//ci ste shes pa dang khyod nyid gnyis kas shes pa zhig na rgyud gnyis su thal bar 'gyur la/khyod nyid sangs rgyas pa'i tshe yang rgyud gnyis su thal bar 'gyur ro//
8b3(mdo sde): des na 'di ltar rtogs par bya ste/khyod kyis mun pa mthong ba nyid las nad gsal bar bsnyad pa'o//ces smra ba 'di ni gnas med do//kun dga' bos gsol ba/bdag gis bcom ldan 'das kyis kun
8b4(mdo sde): du 'khor rnam bzhi la bka' stsal pa thos pa las na shes pa yod pas na shes bya sna tshogs pa yod la/shes bya yod pas na shes pa sna tshogs pa skye bar gsungs pas na/bdag gis 'di ltar sems te//
8b5(mdo sde): sems kyi dngos po 'di nyid ka bdag gi sems kyi rang bzhin lags te/yul dang 'phrad pa na sems rjes su skye ba zhig kho na yin gyi phyi dang nang dang bar na'ang med do//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
8b6(mdo sde): pakhyod kyis shes bya yod pas shes pa sna tshogs pa 'byung la yul dang 'phrad pa na sems rjes su skye bar smra na de lta na shes pa dngos po med pa nyid kyis ji ltar yul dang 'phrad par 'gyur/ci ste shes pa
8b7(mdo sde): dngos po med pa nyid yul dang 'phrad par smra na yul bdun pa dang /khams bcu dgu pa nyid 'phrad pa zhig tu 'gyur la don 'di ni med pa nyid do//'on te shes pa dngos po yod pa nyid na khyod kyi lag pas rang gi
9a1(mdo sde): lus la reg pa nyid na rtogs pa'i sems de nang nas 'byung ba nyid dam/phyi rol nas 'jug pa zhig yin grang /nang nas 'byung ba zhig na yang lus kyi nang nyid gsal bar 'gyur ro//'on
9a2(mdo sde): te phyi rol nas 'jug pa zhig na sngon du rang gi bzhin gsal bar 'gyur ro//kun dga' bos gsol ba/mig nyid kyis mthong bar 'gyur la shes pas ni rtogs par 'gyur mod kyi mig nyid kyis ma yin/
9a3(mdo sde): la/shes pa kho nas mthong ba yang gnas ma yin no//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/gal te mig nyid kyis mthong bar nus pa nyid na khyod nyid khang pa'i nang du 'dug pa'i sgo nyid kyis kyang
9a4(mdo sde): mthong bar 'gyur ram/shi ba'i ro la yang mig gi dbang po snang bas des kyang mthong bar rigs la/des kyang mthong na ni ji ltar shi ba nyid yin/kun dga' bo/gal te rnam par shes pa gsal
9a5(mdo sde): zhing rig pa dngos por smra ba nyid na dngos po ngo bo gcig pa zhig gam/'on te du ma zhig yin grang /da lta khyod kyi lus la khyab pa nyid dam/ma khyab pa'i dngos po zhig yin grang /gal te dngos po
9a6(mdo sde): gcig pa zhig na lag pas yan lag gcig la reg pa na yan lag bzhi po thams cad kyis myong bar rigs la/thams cad kyis myong na ni reg pa nyid mi 'thad par 'gyur ro//reg pa yod na ni ngo bo
9a7(mdo sde): gcig pa mi 'grub bo//gal te du ma zhig yin na ni yang gang zag rgyud du mar 'gyur la/de lta na gang zhig khyod kyi yin par 'gyur/gal te khyab pa zhig yin na ni sngon du reg pa'i tshe brjod pa dang mtshung/
9b1(mdo sde): la gal te ma khyab pa zhig yin na ni khyod kyi dus gcig char mgo bo dang rkang pa la reg pa'i tshe mgo bos ni myong bar 'gyur la/rkang pas ni mi myong bar 'gyur ba zhig na khyod kyi 'di mi 'thad pa zhig go//des
9b2(mdo sde): na 'di ltar rtogs par bya ste/khyod kyis yul dang 'phrad pa na sems rjes su skye bar smras pa 'di ni gnas med do//kun dga' bos gsol pa/ston pa/bdag gis bcom ldan 'das kyis 'jam
9b3(mdo sde): dpal la sogs pa'i rgyal ba'i sras rnams la yang dag pa ji lta ba 'chad pa'i tshe/ston pas/shes pa nang na yang ma yin/phyi rol na yang ma yin/zhes kyang gsungs pa thos pa las na/bdag
9b4(mdo sde): gis 'di ltar bsams te/nang na gsal bar bya ba'ang ma mchis la/phyi rol du phan tshun gsal ba yang ma mchis la/nang du gsal bar byed pa ma mchis pas nang du yod par mi 'grub la//
9b5(mdo sde): lus sems 'brel bas na phyi rol du yang mi 'grub pas/'di ltar na nang du yang gsal bar ma mchis pas dbus nyid na mchis par 'os so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis
9b6(mdo sde): dbus nyid du smras pa de dbus nyid yin na gsal bar gnas pa nyid du mngon pas na khyod kyi dbus nyid gang zhig na mchis/gnas ga ge mo zhig gam/lus nyid na gnas grang /khyod kyi dbus
9b7(mdo sde): nyid ston cig gal te lus nyid nang du gnas pa lta na/de bas na logs shig tu gnas pas dbus nyid ma yin te dbus nyid kyi nang du na lus kyi nang du gnas pa dang mtshungs pa nyid do//'on te
10a1(mdo sde): gnas shig na yod na ni drang thig yod pa zhig gam/drang thig med pa zhig grang /drang thig med pa zhig na gtan nas med pa dang mtshungs so//yod na ni yang drang thig ma nges pa//
10a2(mdo sde): nyid de/ci'i slad du na/dper na/mi 'ga' zhig gis drang thig bslang nas/drang thig dbus su byas te shar nas bltas pa'i tshe nub kyi ngos su 'gyur la/lho nas bltas pa'i tshe byang gi ngos su 'gyur/
10a3(mdo sde): byas drang thig 'chol ba nyid kyis sems kyang 'chol bar 'gyur ro//kun dga' bos gsol ba/bdag gis smras pa'i dbus ni de lta ma lags te/ston pas mig dang gzugs 'dus pa las mi
10a4(mdo sde): gi rnam par shes pa 'byung ngo gsungs pa las na mig gis ni bye brag 'byed par 'gyur la/gzugs ni shes pa dang bral ba ste rnam par shes pa ni de'i dbus nyid nas 'byung bas 'di ni sems kyi
10a5(mdo sde): gnas so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis dbang po dang yul gyi dbus su sems gnas par blta na dbang po yul dang lhan cig pa'am/lhan cig pa ma yin pa zhig yin grang
10a6(mdo sde): lhan cig pa nyid na dbang po dang yul 'chol bar 'gyur te/dbang pos ni rtogs la yul gyis ni ma yin pas/tha dad pa nyid du zad pas na/ji ltar lhan cig pa'i dbus su 'gyur ro//'on te
10a7(mdo sde): gnyis ka lhan cig pa ma yin na ni rtogs pa dang mi rtogs pa med pa nyid kyis dngos po rang bzhin med pa nyid du 'gyur bas dbus na gnas pa ji ltar 'thad par 'gyur/des na 'di ltar rtogs par
10b1(mdo sde): bya ste/dbus na gnas par smra ba 'di ni gnas med do//kun dga' bos gsol ba/ston pa/bdag gis sngon bcom ldan 'das/mod+gal gyi bu chen po dang /rab 'byor dang gang po dang shA ri'i bu ste/
10b2(mdo sde): nyan thos chen po bzhi dang lhan cig chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mthong ba na rtogs cing shes la bye brag phyed pa'i sems kyi rang bzhin nang du yang mi gnas/phyi rol na yang ma yin/dbus na'ang med la/
10b3(mdo sde): gnas med pas na thams cad du thogs pa med do zhes rtag tu gsungs pa thos pa las na/'di ni sems kyi gnas lags te/thams cad du thogs pa med pa 'di nyid ka sems kyi rang bzhin du bsnyad par
10b4(mdo sde): bgyi'am/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyi rnam par shes pa gsal zhing rig pa'i rang bzhin gnas med par smra na/'jig rten na bar snang dang chu dang skam la lding zhing g.yo ba dang brtan
10b5(mdo sde): pa'i dngos po thams cad kyi rnam pa 'di la thams cad zhes bsnyad pa ste/khyod kyi thogs pa med pa 'di la gnas yod pa zhig gam med pa zhig yin grang /gnas med pa zhig na ni rus sbrul gyi spu dang ri bong
10b6(mdo sde): gi rwa dang mtshungs pas ji ltar na yang thogs pa med par smra bar byed/'on te thogs pa med pa 'di yod pa zhig na ni yod pas na ji ltar yang med par gdags par bya rigs/dngos po med pa ni med pa
10b7(mdo sde): nyid yin la med pa ma yin pa ni dngos po yod pa nyid do//dngos po yod pa nyid ni sdod lugs su yod pa ste/ji ltar na thogs pa med par gdags/'di ltar rtogs par bya ste/thams cad du thogs pa med
11a1(mdo sde): pa nyid sems kyi rang bzhin du smras pa 'di ni gnas med do//de'i tshe kun dga' bos dge 'dun gyi dbus su stan las langs te/bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar te/pus mo g.yas//
11a2(mdo sde): pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs nas thal mo sbyar te gus pas btud nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//bdag ni bcom ldan 'das kyi nu bo tha chung lags te/bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs
11a3(mdo sde): brtse bas rjes su bzung ste/da lta rab tu byung nas kyang snying du sdug pa nyid blo ba la bcags shing mang du thos pa lags kyang zag pa zad par ma gyur pas/ka pi la'i rigs sngags bcom zhing gzhig par
11a4(mdo sde): ma nus pas de'i dbang du gyur nas smad 'tshong ma'i gnas su'akhrid par gyur pa lags te/yang dag pa'i mtha' la 'jug pa'i tshul rtogs par ma gyur pas/bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs byams
11a5(mdo sde): pa dang brtse ba chen pos bdag cag rnams la sha ma tha ting nge 'dzin gyi lam rjes su bstan du gsol/log sred can rnams drang du gsol/log par lta ba gzhom du gsol/zhes gsol nas
11a6(mdo sde): yan lag lngas sa la gtugs te phyag 'tshal nas/'khor 'dus pa thams cad dang lhan cig mngon par phyogs te dad pas rtse gcig tu chos 'chad pa la rna ba blags te 'dug go/de'i tshe bcom
11a7(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyi dpral ba nas 'od zer sna tshogs pa kha dog tha dad pa nyi ma brgya stong dang mtshungs pa bkye ste/sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rnam pa drug tu g.yos par gyur pa dang /de bzhin du
11b1(mdo sde): phyogs bcu'i rdul phra rab snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams dus gcig tu gsal bar gyur te/ning thams cad kyang bcom ldan 'das kyi gzi brjid kyi dpal gyis gcig tu mnyam par gyur to//zhing de
11b2(mdo sde): dag thams cad na yang byang chub sems dpa' chen po ji snyed cig yod pa thams cad kyang rang rang gi zhing na 'khod bzhin du thal mo sbyar te chos ston pa la mnyan par sems shing 'dug go//bcom ldan 'das
11b3(mdo sde): kyis kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/sems can rnams thog ma med pa nas shing tog a kra gu dang mtshungs pa'i phyin ci log gi rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i las kyi sa bon dang gis smin pas/kun tu dka'
11b4(mdo sde): thub spyod pa rnams bla na med pa'i byang chub thob par ma nus te/phyir zhing nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang /gzhan yang mu stegs byed dang /lha dang bdud kyi ris kyi dbang po dang /bdud kyi sde thams cad du
11b5(mdo sde): 'jug go//de ni rgyud kyi rnam grangs gnyis mi shes par/gzhan du 'khrul pa la zhugs pa dag/bye ma btsos pa la zas kyi mchog tu 'gyur bar rloms pa dang mtshungs pas/rdul phra rab snyed kyi bskal
11b6(mdo sde): pa'i bar du brtson par byas kyang byang chub 'thob par mi nus so//ji ltar na rnam grangs gnyis yin zhe na/kun dga' bo rnam grangs gcig ni thog ma med pa'i skye 'chi'i rtsa ba ste/da lta khyod cag sems
11b7(mdo sde): can rnams kyi dmigs pa can gyi sems nyid rang gi sems kyi rang bzhin du blta ba'o//rnam grangs gzhan ni/thog ma med pa nas 'bral du med pa'i byang chub dang myang 'das rnam par byang ba'i ngo bo
12a1(mdo sde): nyid de/da lta khyod kyi rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i rnam par shes pa'i khams/rnam 'gyur thams cad bskyed par byed pa/rang gi ngo bo rnyed par dka' ba ste/sems can
12a2(mdo sde): rnams kyis rang gi ngo bo yongs su stor bas na/nyin bzhin du 'bad par byas kyang phyin ci log gi rigs sna tshogs su don med par 'khyams par gyur te rang gi rang bzhin ma rtogs so//kun dga'
12a3(mdo sde): bo da ste ting nge 'dzin gyi lam gyis skye 'chi'i rang bzhin spong bar 'dod na 'di khyod la dri bar bya'o zhes bka' stsal te/de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gser gyi mdog can khu tshur mdzad nas
12a4(mdo sde): brkyang ste/kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis 'di mthong ngam/kun dga' bos gsol pa/mthong lags so//bka' stsal pa/ji ltar mthong ba yin/gsol pa/de bzhin gshegs/
12a5(mdo sde): pa'i khu tshur gser gyi mdog can gyis bdag gi yid dang mig snang bar byas lags so//bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis ci zhig gis mthong /gsol ba/bdag cag 'khor 'dus pas mig gis//
12a6(mdo sde): mthong lags so//bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i khu tshur gser gyi mdog can gyis khyod kyi mig dang yid snang bar byas par smran khyod kyi mig gis mthong mod kyi/khyod
12a7(mdo sde): kyi sems gang zhig bdag gi phyag gis snang bar bgyi ba'i yul du 'gyur/kun dga' bos gsol ba/bcom ldan 'das kyis sems gang du gnas pa 'dri na/bdag gis sems btsal
12b1(mdo sde): te dpyad cing nan tar gtugs pa na dpyod cing gtugs pa 'di ni sems lags so snyam du sems so//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/mthong 'di ni khyod kyi sems ma yin no zhes so//kun
12b2(mdo sde): dga' bo dngangs te/stan las langs te thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/'di nyid bdag gi sems ma yin na ci zhig bdag gi sems yin/bka' stsal pa/'di ni phyi rol don
12b3(mdo sde): gyis stobs pa'i sems kyi rnam pardzun pa ste/yang dag pa'i sems kyi rang bzhin rnyog par byed do//khyod kyis thog ma med pa nas da lta'i bar du rkun po la rang gi bur rloms pas/sems kyi rang
12b4(mdo sde): bzhin gyi ngo bo nyid stor bas na 'khor bar 'khor ro//kun dga' bos gsol ba/ston pa/bdag ni bcom ldan 'das kyi nu bo tha chung lags te/bdag gis bcom ldan 'das la mngon par dad
12b5(mdo sde): pas rab tu byung ste/bdag gis bcom ldan 'das nyid la bsnyen bkur ba nas/gang+gA'i bye ma snyed kyi zhing khams kyi mthar thug pa'i bcom ldan 'das bshes gnyen la dge ba'i rtsa ba bsgrub pa'i
12b6(mdo sde): snying stobs chen po bskyed de bya bar dka' ba'i spyod pa spyad pa mtha' dag sems 'di kho na'i bgyi ba lags so//dam pa'i chos la skur pa 'debs shing dge ba'i rtsa ba smad par byed pa rnams kyang sems
12b7(mdo sde): 'di nyid lags so//da lta rnam par dpyod pa'i sems 'di nyid ma yin par gsungs na da ni sems nyid med par 'gyur te/sa dang shing lta bur 'gyur ro//sems gsal ba nyid dang bral na ni
13a1(mdo sde): gzhan ci zhig yod par 'gyur/bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na 'di ltar gsungs te/'di sems nyid ma yin par gsungs te/bdag dngangs par ma zad nyan thos 'di dag kyang //
13a2(mdo sde): the tshom med pa ma mchis so//thugs rje chen pos bdag cag gi rmongs pa bsal du gsol/de'i tshe ston pas kun dga' bo/nyan thos kyi 'khor 'dus pa dang bcas par thams cad kyang mi skye
13a3(mdo sde): ba'i chos la bzod pa thob par bya ba'i phyir yongs su 'chad par mdzad pas/bcom ldan 'das seng ge'i khri la bzhugs pa nyid kyis kun dga' bo'i spyi bor phyag bzhag ste bka' stsal pa/bcom
13a4(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyis kun du 'chad pa na/chos thams cad kyi 'byung ba ni/sems las 'byung ba ste/'jig rten na rdul phra rab yan chad kyi rgyu dang 'bras bu thams cad kyang sems kyi rgyu las dngos
13a5(mdo sde): por red par bshad de/kun dga' bo 'jig rten na yod pa'i chos thams cad kyi nang na rtswa dang lo ma dang snal ma dang 'jur mdud yan chad kyang rgyu'i rnam pa dang bcas pa ste/stong pa'i ngo bo dag kyang
13a6(mdo sde): ming dang rnam pa dang bcas so//'od gsal ba'i sems rmad du byung ba rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i sems kyi khams ni ji ltar na dngos po med par 'gyur/gal te khyod kyis ci nas rnam par 'byed pa rtogs
13a7(mdo sde): cing dpyod pa'i sems kun du gsal ba 'di nyid ka sems kyi bdag nyid du mngon par zhen na/de lta na gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg bya sogs las su bya ba'i yul thams cad dang bral ba'i gzhan/
13b1(mdo sde): du sems kyi dngos po yongs su rdzogs pa zhig yod par 'gyur ro//da lta khyod kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi chos 'chad pa nyan pa na rnam par 'byed pa'i rtog pa 'di ni chos kyi sgra nyid las 'byung zhing /phyi rol
13b2(mdo sde): gyi gzugs dang sgra yongs su chad pa'i zhi ba'i sems kho nar yongs su brtags par gnas pa na yang chos kyi yul gyis bcings te/rdul gyi gzugs brnyan la rnam par dpyod pa dang 'dra ste/bdag
13b3(mdo sde): gis khyod la sems med par blta bar bshad pa ma yin te/gzhan du na khyod kyis sems nyid la so sor rtog pas dpyod par gyis shig/gal te yul gyi rnam pa dang bral ba'i rnam par 'byed pa'i
13b4(mdo sde): sems nyid ka khyod kyi sems yin na/rnam par 'byed pa'i sems yul gyi rnam pa dang bral ba ni dngos po med par 'gyur la/'on te 'di nyid ka yul gyi rnam pa rnam par rig pa'i rdul gyi gzugs
13b5(mdo sde): brnyan dang 'dra na yul ni mi rtag pa ste/de nyid 'gag pa'i dus su phyin pa na sems nyid rus sbal gyi spu dang ri bong gi rwa dang mtshungs par 'gyur ro//khyod kyi chos nyid kyi sku dang lhan cig chad pa dang 'gag
13b6(mdo sde): par 'gyur bas gang zhig gis skye ba med pa'i chos la bzod par 'gyur/de'i tshe kun dga' bo 'khor 'dus pa dang bcas pa cang mi smra bar ngo mtshar zhing 'khod do//bcom ldan 'das kyis kun dga' bo la/
13b7(mdo sde): bka' stsal pa/'jig rten na lam yongs su slob pa rnams da lta mthar gyis snyoms 'jug dgu la bslab kyang zag pa zad pa'i dgra bcom par mi 'gyur te skye 'chi'i rnam par rtog pa sems nyid la
14a1(mdo sde): bden par rloms pas so//de yang kun dga' bo khyod kyang mang du thos pa nyid na'ang 'phags pa'i 'bras bu thob par ma gyur to//kun dga' bos de skad thos pa dang yang mchi ma
14a2(mdo sde): blags te/yan lag lngas sa la gtugs nas/pus mo btsugs te thal mo sbyar nas/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/bdag gis ston pa'i zham 'bring bar rab tu byung nas/ston pa'i
14a3(mdo sde): gzi byin gyi mthu las/rtag tu bsam pa na bdag gis yongs su 'bad pa med par ci zhig nas bcom ldan 'das kyis ting nge 'dzin bskal bar bgyid do snyam du sems lags te/lus sems
14a4(mdo sde): tha dad du yongs su ma rtogs lags pas/bdag gi sems kyi de kho na nyid stor bar gyur na lus kyis tshangs par spyad na'ang sems kyis 'bras bu mngon du ma byas te/dper na bu dbul po rang
14a5(mdo sde): gi pha bsgyur te bros pa bzhin no//dra ste mang du thos na'ang bsgom pas yid la ma byas na ni ma thos pa dang mtshungs par 'gyur te/gzhan gyis zas bzang por bsnyad kyang ro ma myong ba bzhin no//ston
14a6(mdo sde): pabadog cag ni da lta sgrib pa gnyis kyis bcings pas/sems kyi de kho na nyid rtogs par ma gyur lags te/bcom ldan 'das bdag cag mgon med skyabs med rnams la thugs brtse
14a7(mdo sde): bas sems kyi de kho na nyid gsal bar mdzad cing chos kyi mig 'byed par mdzad du gsol/ces gsol pa dang /de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs kyi mdapal be'u las 'od zer gyi tshogs
14b1(mdo sde): kha dog brgya stong 'khrug pa spros te/phyogs bcu'i rdul phra rab snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad dus gcig tu bskor te/zhing bkod pa de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi gtsug tor la reg nas slar 'khyil te/
14b2(mdo sde): kun dga' bo dang 'khor 'dus pa rnams kyang snang bar byas so//kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/bdag gis khyod kyi slad du chos kyi rgyal mtshan chen po bsgreng zhing /phyogs bcu'i sems can thams
14b3(mdo sde): tsha la yang zab cing gsang 'i'i de kho na nyid dang dag cing gsal ba'i sems kyi rang bzhin gsal bar byed cing rnam par dag pa'i mig 'thob par byas so//kun dga' bo/khyod kyis snar lan gsol
14b4(mdo sde): pa'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag 'od 'phro ba'i khu tshur rgyu cis na yod par smra/ji ltar na khu tshur du grub/ci zhig gis mthong bar gyur/kun dga' bos gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das kyi sku dza m+bu chu ra re
14b5(mdo sde): gser gyi mdog can rin po che'i ri bo dang mtshungs pa dag cing gsal bar 'khrungs pas na 'od zer gyis rgyas lags te/bdag cag gi mig lam du snang ba na/phyag sor gyi 'khor lo rnam par bzlum
14b6(mdo sde): teston par mdzad pa las na khu tshur gyi rnam par snang ngo //bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/bcom ldan 'das kyis da ste bde ba'i bka' yis gsol bar bgyi ste/blo gros dang ldan pa rnams ni
14b7(mdo sde): dpes bsnyad pa na rtogs par 'gyur te/kun dga' bo dper na bcom ldan 'das kyi khu tshur ni bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag ma mchis na bcom ldan 'das kyi khu tshur du mi 'grub la/khyod kyi mig ma mchis/
15a1(mdo sde): na khyod kyi mthong bar mi 'grub ste/khyod kyi mig gi dbang po bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag dang dper bgyis pa na 'dra bar mchis sam/kun dga' bos gsol pa/de de bzhin te/
15a2(mdo sde): ston pa/bdag gi mig gi dbang po dang bral nA ni bdag gis mthong bar mi 'grub ste/bdag gi mig gi dbang po bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag dang dper bgyis pa ni don mtshungs pa lags so//
15a3(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis 'dra bar bsnyad pa ni/don 'dra ba ma yin te/ci'i phyir na/lag pa med pa'i mi la khu tshur nyid med par rigs te/dper na mig med pa'i mis

28b1(mdo sde): pa gsob dang rdzun dang phyin ci log thams cad dang yongs su bral ba 'di ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ma yin pa lta na/de dag gis rang byung du grub ces smras pa dang 'dra bas ji ltar na rnam par phye ste/

28b3(mdo sde): pa/kun dga' bo/bdag gis da lta de lta bur thabs la mkhas pas phye ste bstan nas khyod la yang dag par bka' stsal pa na/khyod kyis ma rtogs par rang byung ba'o snyam du rtog go//kun dga'

28b5(mdo sde): 'di'i nang na gang zhig bdag yin/mthong ba 'di'i snang ba bdag gam/mun pa bdag gam/stong pa bdag gam/bem po bdag yin/kun dga' bo/gal te snang ba bdag yin na mun pa mi
28b6(mdo sde): mthong bar 'gyur ro//gal te stong pa rang byung ba'i dngos po yin na bem po mi mthong bar 'gyur ro//de bzhin du des mtshon nas mun pa'i mtshan ma la sogs pa'i bar bdag yin na/snang ba'i dus su

29a1(mdo sde): par bka' stsal pa las na/yang bdag gis gsal bar rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yin snyam du sems so//'on kyang ji lta ba bzhin legs par ma rtogs pas de bzhin

29a6(mdo sde): ngam mun pa dang 'brel bar mthong ngam/stong pa dang 'brel bar mthong ngam/bem po dang 'bral bar mthong /kun dga' bo/gal te stong pa dang 'brel pa yin na bem po mi mthong bar rigs
29a7(mdo sde): so/bem po dang 'brel pa yin na stong pa mi mthong bar rigs so//de bzhin du snang ba dang 'brel ba dang mun pa dang 'brel ba'i bar du stong pa dang bem po ltar ro//'di ltar rig par bya ste/yang dag
29b1(mdo sde): cing rmad du blang ba gsal zhing rig pa 'di gdod ma nas rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yang ma yin/rang byung du grub pa yang ma yin/rang byung du ma grub pa yang ma yin/ma yin pa yang ma yin/ma yin pa
29b2(mdo sde): min pa yang ma yin/yin pa yang ma yin/yin pa min pa yang ma yin zhing mtshan ma thams cad dang bral ba'i de kho na nyid ni chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin no//khyod da lta ci'i phyir 'di la sems zhen

30a2(mdo sde): nyi ma dang zla ba dang sgron me'i 'od la brten nas dngos po sna tshogs mthong bas na mthong ba zhes bya la/gal te 'od gsal ba'i snang ba gsum po 'di med na mthong bar mi nus so//kun dga' bo//gal

31a2(mdo sde): rgyas par bka' stsal par dgongs te kun dga' bo la 'di skad ces bka' stsal pa/kun dga' bo khyod kyis nan tan du sbyangs pas mang du thos par gyur mod kyi/don 'di zab cing phra ba'i sgrom byung

33a1(mdo sde): pa mthong ngo zhes bya'o//ci'i phyir yang rig pa dang thos pa dang shes pa dang mthong ba po zhes tha snyad 'dogs par 'gyur/de'i phyir da lta khyod kyis nga dang khyod la sogs pa

34b1(mdo sde): pa 'di mun pa la ltos pa ma yin pa'i phyir ci ltar mun pa mthong bar 'gyur/gal te mun pa mthong ba'i tshe mun pa la ltos pa ma yin gyi snang ba la ltos pa yin snyam na de'i tshe snang ba mthong ba ma yin
34b2(mdo sde): pas/snang ba mi mthong na ci ltar snang ba la ltos zhes brjod par rigs/des snang ba mun pa ma yin pa yang shes sla la/mun pa dang thigs med dang bem po la sogs pa de dag kyang de nyid dang 'dra'o///
34b3(mdo sde): de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang /kun dga' bos bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/bcom ldan 'das/bdag gis 'tshal ba ltar na rmad du byung ba'i gdod ma'i rigs pa 'di dang /yul gyi rkyen
34b4(mdo sde): thams cad dang /sems dang yid dang rnam par shes pa thams cad 'phrad pa dang ltos pa ma yin lags grang zhes gsol ba dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/khyod kyis da dung

35a1(mdo sde): pa'i bar yul gyi mtshams ji ltar 'byed/kun dga' bo gal te snang ba'i nang du nges par mthong ba med ce na de gnyis lhan cig mi gnas pa'i phyir/rang gi snang bar

35a4(mdo sde): byagal te snang ba la ltos pa ma yin zhe na mthong ba dang snang ba'i rang bzhin so sor tha dad du 'gyur ba'i phyir/rna ba snang ba dang phan tshun ltos med don gzhan yin pa bzhin du mthong ba yang

35a6(mdo sde): dga' bo/khyod yang yul kun rdzob pa thams cad dang sgyu ma dang sprul pa la sogs pa'i mtshan ma de nyid las skye zhing /de nyid du 'gag cing zhi ba ma shes so//sgyu mardzun pa la mtshan ma zhes
35a7(mdo sde): tha snyad 'dogs te/de'i rang bzhin nges par rmad du byung ba'i gsal zhing rig pa'o//'di nas phung po lnga dang /skye mched drug dang /gzung 'dzin bcu gnyis dang /khams bco brgyad kyi
35b1(mdo sde): par thams cad kun rdzob tsam du rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba dang 'phrad pa dang ltos pa'i rkyen gyis skyes pa zhes bya ba dang /kun rdzob tsam du rten cing 'byung ba dang bral ba'i rkyen gyis 'gag pa'i ming can du/
35b2(mdo sde): 'gyur ro//mdor na skye 'gag 'gro 'ong ni gdod ma nas de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi ther zug tu gnas pa rnam par dag pa g.yo ba med pa khyab par rdzogs pa de bzhin nyid dam pa'i rang bzhin

36a1(mdo sde): te stong pa de stong pa ma yin zhe na/rang gi ra ri'i mtshan ma de dag rang bzhin gyis spros pa dang zhi ba'i go skabs med pa'i phyir/kun dga' bo'i lus la lus de nyid thim par

36a3(mdo sde): mthong ba yod par rigs so//gal te mthong ba yod cen nam mkha' la song nas ra rir gyur pa yin na tshur la mig mthong bar rigs so//gal te mthong ba med ce na nam mkha' la song ste rab

36b3(mdo sde): byung ba yin zhe na/sbyor mi dgos so//gzhan yang thal mo las byung ba yin pas sbyar ba na thal mos tshor dgos so//phye ba na reg pa thim par 'gyur zhe na/dpung pa dang lag ngar dang rus pa dang

37a1(mdo sde): kha la zhugs pa ma yin no//kun dga' bo 'di ltar rig par bya ste/gal te shing thog skyur po las byung ba yin zhe na/shing thog rang nyid kyis smra bar rigs kyi/skye bos sgrub

40b7(mdo sde): ma thag tu 'gag pa'i phyir bral ba ji ltar shes par 'gyur/phan pa dang gnod pa'i mtshan ma gnyis de nyid dang 'dra'o//gal te dbang po las byung ba yin zhe na/gdon mi za bar 'bral ba
41a1(mdo sde): dang 'phrad pa dang phan pa dang gnod pa'i mtshan ma bzhi med par 'gyur ro//'di ltar na khyod kyi lus kyi shes pa gdod ma nas rang bzhin med do//gdon mi za bar stong pa las

41a3(mdo sde): 'byung ba ma yin/rang byung ba'i rang bzhin yang ma yin zhes shes par bya'o//kun dga' bo dper na skye bo gang zhig ngal zhing dub nas gnyid log log pa las sad par 'gyur ba dang yul mthong
41a4(mdo sde): zhing sems kyi kun rtog 'char la sems g.yengs nas 'phral du brjed pa dang 'dra/de ltar log par rtog pas rim bzhin du skye ba dang /gnas pa dang /'pho ba dang /'gag pa'i bag chags smin/
41a5(mdo sde): pa myong ba'i dbang gis rim pa mi 'chol bar 'byung ba ni yid kyi shes pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o//yid dang bcas pa ngal ba'i 'khrul pa thams cad byang chub kyi chos nyid kyis gtad nas ngal zhing
41a6(mdo sde): 'khrul ba'i mtshan ma yin zhing /skye 'gag gnyis bden pa ma yin pa'i yul la brten nas par skabs der shes pa 'dus te/mthong ba dang thos pa nang du log nas 'jug tu med pa'i yul
41a7(mdo sde): skye zhing 'gag pa'i nang gi don myong ba'i phyir shes pa'i rang bzhin zhes gdags so//shes pa'i rang bzhin 'di sad gnyid dang /skye 'gag ste yul de gnyis dang bral ba na gtan nas med do//
41b1(mdo sde): kun dga' bo 'di ltar rig par bya ste/shes pa'i dbang po 'di sad pa dang gnyid log pa las byung ba ma yin/skye 'gag las byung ba ma yin/dbang po las byung ba ma yin/stong pa las byung ba
41b2(mdo sde): yang ma yin no//de ci'i phyir zhe na/gal te sad pa las byung ba yin na/gnyid log nas 'phral du 'gag pa'i phyir gang zhig gnyid log pa yin zhes bya/gdon mi za bar skyes pa'i tshe byung ba yin//
41b3(mdo sde): zhe na/'gag na med pa nyid dang 'dra/'gag pa su zhig gis tshor/gal te 'gag pa las byung ba yin zhe na/skyes pas 'gag pa gtan nas med cing /skyes pa shes pa po su zhig/gal te
41b4(mdo sde): dbang po las byung ba yin zhe na/sad pa dang gnyid log pa'i mtshan ma gnyis lus kyi dbang gis 'byed pa dang sdud par 'gyur ro//dngos po 'di gnyis dang bral ba na de shes pa'i shes pa nam
41b5(mdo sde): mkha'i me tog bzhin gtan nas rang bzhin med do//gal te stong pa las byung ba yin zhe na/stong pa rang nyid shes pa por 'gyur bas khyod kyi skye mched la ltos pa 'brel med do//de'i phyir yid kyi
41b6(mdo sde): skye mched kun rdzob tsam yin zhing /gdod ma nas rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ma yin/rang byung ba'i rang bzhin ma yin zhes shes par bya'o//slar yang kun dga' bo ji ltar na skye mched bcu
41b7(mdo sde): gnyis gdod ma nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po dam pa'i rang bzhin yin zhe na/kun dga' bo khyod kyi da lta ltos shig/dze ta'i tshal 'di dang /yang chu mig dang rdzing bu la sogs pa sna
42a1(mdo sde): tshogs su mthong ba 'di ji snyam du sems/'di dag gzugs las mig gi yul du gyur pa yin zhe'am/mig las gzugs kyi mtshan mar gyur pa yin zhe'am/kun

42b1(mdo sde): 'ongs pa yin snyam mam/rna ba sgra'i gnas su song ba yin snyam mam/kun dga' bo gal te sgra 'di rna ba'i drung du 'ongs pa yin zhe na/dper na nga mnyan yod kyi grong khyer du bsod snyoms la phyin pa na ji
42b2(mdo sde): tati'i tshal dung med pa dang 'dra/sgra 'di gdon mi za bar kun dga' bo'i rna ba la 'ongs pa'i phyir/mot+pal gyi bu dang 'od srungs la sogs pa thams cad kyi rna bar mi thos par rigs na/'di'i nang du dge
42b3(mdo sde): slong stong nyis brgya lnga bcu po dag dril chen gyi sgra thos ma thag tu thams cad lhan cig tu bkad sar 'dus nas 'ong ba lta ci smos/slar yang khyod kyi rna ba sgra de'i gnas su song ba yin zhe na/dper na rje
42b4(mdo sde): ta'i tshal du 'ongs nas 'dug pa na nga mnyan yod kyi grong khyer du med pa dang 'dra/khyod kyis rnga'i sgra thos nas rna ba 'phral du rje brdung ba'i sar song ba'i phyir/mnyam du byung ba'i dril chen gyi sgra mi thos par
42b5(mdo sde): rigs na/de'i nang du glang po che dang rta dang phyugs dang lug la sogs pa sna tshogs pa'i sgra skad rnams lta ci smos/gal te 'gro ba dang 'ong ba nyid med na yang thos pa nyid med do//de'i phyir thos pa dang
42b6(mdo sde): sgra'i gdangs thams cad gnas kyang med/thos pa dang yul sgra gnyis kun rdzob tsam yin zhing /gdod ma nas rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yang ma yin/rang byung ba'i rang bzhin yang ma yin zhes
42b7(mdo sde): shes par bya'o//kun dga' bo yang khyod spos snod kyi nang du bsreg pa'i tsan dan gyi dri la snom zhig/can dan 'di las cung zad cig bsregs pa na mnyan yod kyi grong khyer gyi mtha' skor kun nas rgyang
43a1(mdo sde): grags bzhi bcu'i nang du dus gcig tu thams cad kyis dri tshor bar 'gyur ro//'di ji snyam du sems tsan dan gyi dri 'di tsan dan gyi shing las skyes pa yin snyam mam/khyod kyi sna/
43a2(mdo sde): las skyes pa yin snyam mam/yang na stong pa las skyes pa yin snyam mam/kun dga' bo gal te tsan dan gyi dri 'di khyod kyi sna las skyes pa yin zhe na/sna las skyes pa de nyid sna las 'byung bar
43a3(mdo sde): rigs na sna de tsan dan ma yin no//ci'i phyir sna'i nang du tsan dan gyi dri yod par 'gyur/khyod kyis tsan dan gyi dri tshor ro zhe na/snar 'jug par rigs pas sna'i nang nas tsan dan gyi dri byung ba la tsher ro/

43a5(mdo sde): po 'di bsreg ci dgos/gal te shing las skyes pa yin zhe na/ci'i phyir tsan dan bsreg pa 'di las da gdod du ba byung ba yin/snas tshor ro zhe na/ci'i phyir du ba'i dri la smug dgos/du ba de
43a6(mdo sde): nam mkha' la song nas thag ring por ma phyin pa la/rgyang grag bzhi bcu'i bar du thams cad kyis ji ltar dri tshor bar 'gyur/de'i phyir tsan dan dang snas dri snom pa thams cad gnas kyang med///
43a7(mdo sde): snom pa dang yul dri gnyis kun rdzob tsam yin zhing /gdod ma nas rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yang ma yin/rang byung ba'i rang bzhin yang ma yin zhes shes par bya'o//kun dga' bo khyod
43b1(mdo sde): dusu gnyis su tshogs mang po dang mnyam du bsod snyoms la 'gro bar 'gyur la/de ltar 'gro ba na 'ga' zhig tu zho 'o ma mar khu bdud rtsi lta bu rnyed nas zos te/ro mchog zhes tha skad 'dogs so//
43b2(mdo sde): 'di ji snyam du sems/ro 'di stong pa las skyes pa yin snyam mam/lce las skyes pa yin snyam mam/yang na zas las skyes pa yin snyam mam/kun dga' bo gal te ro 'di khyod kyi lce las/

43b4(mdo sde): gyur pa de nyid la ro shes pa zhes brjod du mi rung ngo //gzhan du 'gyur na lce mang po ma yin pa'i phyir/ji ltar lce gcig gis ro de snyed cig shes par 'gyur/gal te zas las skyes pa yin zhe na//

43b6(mdo sde): pa yin zhe na/nam mkha' stong pa'i ro myong bar gyis shig dang ro ji ltar 'dug/gdon mi za bar nam mkha' stong pa'i ro de lan tshwa'i ro'o zhe na/khyod kyi lces lan tshwa'i ro myong bar 'gyur zhing /

44a1(mdo sde): 'gyur ro//ro mi bro ba mi shes na lan tshwa'i ro mi tshor bar 'gyur ro//gdon mi za bar shes pa med ce na/ji ltar ro zhes tha snyad 'dogs/de'i phyir ro dang lce dang bro ba thams/

44a7(mdo sde): reg byed la yod na reg bya ma yin/reg bya la yod na reg byed ma yin/stong pa de khyod kyi reg byar mi rigs so//de'i phyir shes pa dang reg bya lus thams cad gnas kyang med/lus dang
44b1(mdo sde): yul reg bya gnyis kun rdzob tsam yin zhing /gdod ma nas rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yang ma yin/rang byung ba'i rang bzhin kyang ma yin zhes shes par bya'o//kun dga' bo khyod kyi sems rgyud

45a1(mdo sde): gnas gang la brten nas gnas/de'i phyir chos kyi gnas lugs dang sems thams cad gnas kyang med/sems dang yul chos gnyis kun rdzob tsam yin zhing //

47a2(mdo sde): dri zhim po yin nam dri nga ba yin/dri nga ba yin na dri zhim po ma yin par 'gyur ro//dri zhim po yin na dri nga ba ma yin par 'gyur ro//gal te dri bzang ngan gnyis po thams cad snom nus na/khyod mi
47a3(mdo sde): gcig la sna gnyis 'byung bar rigs/nga las chos dris pa po'i kun dga' bo gnyis yod pas gang zhig khyod kyi lus su byung ba yin/gal te sna gcig yin zhe na/dri bzang ngan gnyis med
47a4(mdo sde): par 'gyur bar rigs/dri nga ba yang dri zhim por 'gyur ba dang dri zhim po yang dri nga bar 'gyur na/rang bzhin gnyis med pa la khams gang la brten nas gnas/gal te dri las byung ba yin zhe na//

107a7(mdo sde): par byed//gang zhig chu yi rang bzhin la rtogs na//bsam pa'i dmigs pa yang dag don ma yin//gdod ma'i rang bzhin rtog ge'i yul ma yin//ji ltar mngon par byang chub 'grub par
107b1(mdo sde): byed/gang dag me yi rang bzhin la rtog na//sred bral yang dag don la bral ba min//gsar bu bkri ba'i thabs mkhas ma yin phyir//ji ltar mngon par byang chub 'grub par byed//gang dag

107b5(mdo sde): nas skye 'gag ldan//rgyu 'bras so sor ma 'dres pa nyid phyir//ji ltar mngon par byang chub 'grub par byed//deng bdag bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba ni//ston pa mi mjed 'jig rten khams
107b6(mdo sde): 'dir 'khrungs//phyogs 'di'i yang dag bstan pa'i gzhung lugs ni//rnam dag bshad dang nyan pa la ni gnas//gang dag ting 'dzin thob par 'dod pa des//nges par thos pa nyid las yang/

108a2(mdo sde): rlabs kyi dbyangs dang ldan//'jig rten thams cad bskyab cing bde bar mdzad//'jig rten las 'das rtag pa'i gnas su bkod//deng bdag de bzhin gshegs la gsol ba ni//spyan ras

189b7(mdo sde): dang rtsa ba'i ltung ba bcu la spyad nas/dbugs 'byung 'jug tsam du 'jig rten gyi khams 'di dang gzhan gyi mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal bar skye zhing /de nas kyang phyogs bcu'i mnar med pa'i sems can
